Source Code

These source-code files were transcribed from scans made from Don Eyles's personal copy of Luminary 069. They were scanned at archive.org's Boston facility, and the scanning was sponsored by Onno Hommes. The code was transcribed from these scans by a team of volunteers who are referenced in the program comments. Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". In some cases, where similar code blocks exist in previously-transcribed AGC programs (primarily Luminary 99, from Apollo 11) those code blocks were used as a starting point and then corrected to agree with the Luminary 69 scans. The full scans are available at the Virtual AGC project's collection at archive.org, while more-convenient reduced-size (but reduced-quality) images are available at the main Virtual AGC website. Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 069 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-011
	19:02 NOV. 25,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

017503,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
017504,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
017505,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     The main source file for Luminary revision 069.
017506,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the original release
017507,000006:                                                                                                  ##              of the flight software for the Lunar Module's (LM) Apollo
017508,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10. The actual flown
017509,000008:                                                                                                  ##              version was Luminary 69 revision 2, which included a
017510,000009:                                                                                                  ##              newer lunar gravity model and only affected module 2.
017511,000010:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except

017513,000012:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
017514,000013:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
017515,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 403-484

017536,000035:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
017537,000036:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
017538,000037:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
017539,000038:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME  BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
017540,000039: 
017541,000040:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
017542,000041: 
017543,000042:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
017544,000043:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
017545,000044:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
017546,000045:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
017547,000046:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
017548,000047:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
017549,000048:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
017550,000049:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
017551,000050:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
017552,000051: 
017553,000052:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
017554,000053:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
017555,000054:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
017556,000055:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
017557,000056:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
017558,000057:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
017559,000058:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

017594,000093: 
017595,000094:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
017596,000095: 
017597,000096:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
017598,000097:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
017599,000098:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
017600,000099:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
017601,000100:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017602,000101: 
017603,000102:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
017604,000103:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
017605,000104:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
017606,000105:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017607,000106: 
017608,000107:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
017609,000108:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
017610,000109:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
017611,000110:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
017612,000111:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017613,000112: 
017614,000113:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
017615,000114:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
017616,000115:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
017617,000116:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 404 

017619,000118:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
017620,000119:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
017621,000120:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
017622,000121:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
017623,000122:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
017624,000123:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
017625,000124:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
017626,000125:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
017627,000126:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
017628,000127:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
017629,000128: 
017630,000129:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
017631,000130:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
017632,000131:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017633,000132: 
017634,000133: 
017635,000134:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
017636,000135: 
017637,000136:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
017638,000137:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
017639,000138:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
017640,000139: 
017641,000140:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
017642,000141:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
017643,000142:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
017644,000143:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
017645,000144:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
017646,000145:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
017647,000146:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
017648,000147: 
017649,000148:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
017650,000149:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017651,000150: 
017652,000151: 
017653,000152:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
017654,000153: 
017655,000154:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
017656,000155:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
017657,000156:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
017658,000157:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
017659,000158: 
017660,000159: 
017661,000160:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
017662,000161: 
017663,000162:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
017664,000163:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.   REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
017665,000164:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
017666,000165:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
017667,000166: 
017668,000167:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 405 

017670,000169:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
017671,000170: 
017672,000171: 
017673,000172:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
017674,000173: 
017675,000174:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
017676,000175:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
017677,000176: 
017678,000177:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
017679,000178:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
017680,000179:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
017681,000180:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
017682,000181: 
017683,000182:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
017684,000183:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
017685,000184: 
017686,000185:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
017687,000186:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
017688,000187:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
017689,000188:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
017690,000189: 
017691,000190:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
017692,000191:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
017693,000192: 
017694,000193:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
017695,000194:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
017696,000195: 
017697,000196:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
017698,000197: 
017699,000198:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
017700,000199:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
017701,000200:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
017702,000201:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017703,000202: 
017704,000203:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
017705,000204:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017706,000205: 
017707,000206:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
017708,000207:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
017709,000208: 
017710,000209: 
017711,000210:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
017712,000211:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
017713,000212:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017714,000213:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

017732,000231: 
017733,000232:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
017734,000233: 
017735,000234: 
017736,000235:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017737,000236: 
017738,000237:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT ERASE                  DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
017739,000238:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH ERASE                  +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
017740,000239:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG  ERASE                  VERB CODE
017741,000240:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG  ERASE                  NOUN CODE
017742,000241:                                                                                                  #  XREG     ERASE                  R1 INPUT BUFFER
017743,000242:                                                                                                  #  YREG     ERASE                  R2 INPUT BUFFER
017744,000243:                                                                                                  #  ZREG     ERASE                  R3 INPUT BUFFER
017745,000244:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017746,000245:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017747,000246:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT =      YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017748,000247:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
017749,000248:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017750,000249:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT =      ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017751,000250:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
017752,000251:                                                                                                  #  MODREG   ERASE                  MODE CODE
017753,000252:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK  ERASE                  KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
017754,000253:                                                                                                  #  REQRET   ERASE                  RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
017755,000254:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT ERASE                  STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
017756,000255:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS   ERASE                  PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
017757,000256:                                                                                                  #  NOUT     ERASE                  ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
017758,000257:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR ERASE                  MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
017759,000258:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE  ERASE                  N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
017760,000259:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 ERASE                  NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) =MONSAVE+1
017761,000260:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2 ERASE                  NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017762,000261:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB   ERASE          +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13,C RELAYS
017763,000262:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR ERASE                  ENDIDLE STORAGE
017764,000263:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM   ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
017765,000264:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
017766,000265:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
017767,000266:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVQTEM+1
017768,000267:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE ERASE                  NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
017769,000268:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST  ERASE                  WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
017770,000269:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT REASE                  EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
017771,000270:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
017772,000271:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
017773,000272:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017774,000273:

017799,000298:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP   =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
017800,000299:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1  =      VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART(=SFTEMP2-1)
017801,000300:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN  =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017802,000301:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
017803,000302:                                                                                                  #  CODE     =      VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
017804,000303:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2  =      VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART(=SFTEMP1+1)
017805,000304:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN  =      VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017806,000305:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMIN+1.
017807,000306:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP  =      VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
017808,000307:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET  =      VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
017809,000308: 
017810,000309:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
017811,000310: 
017812,000311:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET   =      DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
017813,000312: 
017814,000313:                                                                                                  #  WDCNT    =      DOTRET          CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD

2003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

017893,000392: 
017894,000393: 
017895,000394:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
017896,000395:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
017897,000396:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
017898,000397:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
017899,000398:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
017900,000399:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
017901,000400: 
017902,000401:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
017903,000402:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
017904,000403:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
017905,000404:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
017906,000405:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
017907,000406:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
017908,000407: 
017909,000408:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
017910,000409:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1  11         ALL ARE OCTAL
017911,000410:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2  10
017912,000411:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3   7
017913,000412:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4   6
017914,000413:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5   5
017915,000414:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1   4
017916,000415:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2   3
017917,000416:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3   2
017918,000417:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4   1
017919,000418:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5   0
017920,000419:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
017921,000420: 
017922,000421: 
017923,000422:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
017924,000423: 
017925,000424:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
017926,000425:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
017927,000426:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
017928,000427:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
017929,000428:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
017930,000429:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)

Page 410 

017932,000431:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
017933,000432:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
017934,000433:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
017935,000434:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
017936,000435:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
017937,000436:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
017938,000437:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
017939,000438:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
017940,000439: 
017941,000440: 
017942,000441:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
017943,000442:                                                                                                  #  BLANK      00000
017944,000443:                                                                                                  #  0          10101
017945,000444:                                                                                                  #  1          00011
017946,000445:                                                                                                  #  2          11001
017947,000446:                                                                                                  #  3          11011
017948,000447:                                                                                                  #  4          01111
017949,000448:                                                                                                  #  5          11110
017950,000449:                                                                                                  #  6          11100
017951,000450:                                                                                                  #  7          10011
017952,000451:                                                                                                  #  8          11101
017953,000452:                                                                                                  #  9          11111
017954,000453: 
017955,000454: 
017956,000455:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
017957,000456: 
017958,000457:                                                                                                  #             KEY RELEASE LIGHT    - BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
017959,000458:                                                                                                  #             VERB/NOUN FLASH      - BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
017960,000459:                                                                                                  #             OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT - BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11

018668,001167: 41,2352           61420                           CADR     DSPALARM                              
018669,001168:

Page 426 

018671,001170:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
018672,001171:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
018673,001172:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
018674,001173:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
018675,001174:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
018676,001175:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
018677,001176: 
018678,001177:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
018679,001178:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
018680,001179: 
018681,001180:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
018682,001181: 
018683,001182:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
018684,001183:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
018685,001184:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
018686,001185: 
018687,001186:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018688,001187:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
018689,001188:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018690,001189:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018691,001190:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018692,001191:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
018693,001192: 
018694,001193:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
018695,001194:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
018696,001195:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
018697,001196:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
018698,001197:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
018699,001198: 
018700,001199:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
018701,001200:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
018702,001201:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
018703,001202:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018704,001203:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
018705,001204:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018706,001205:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018707,001206:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018708,001207: 
018709,001208: 
018710,001209:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
018711,001210:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
018712,001211:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
018713,001212: 
018714,001213: 
018715,001214:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
018716,001215:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
018717,001216: 
018718,001217:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
018719,001218:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
018720,001219:

Page 427

019039,001538:                                                                                                  #  BLANKED). THE INTEGER IN THE LOWER NUMBERED ADDRESS IS DISPLAYED IN
019040,001539:                                                                                                  #  RXD1-RXD2.

019044,001543: 40,2734           30154                           CA       MPAC                                  
019045,001544: 40,2735           03306                           TC       DSPDECVN                              #  DISPLAY 1ST INTEGER (LIKE VERB AND NOUN)

019047,001546: 40,2737           50117                           INDEX    DECOUNT                               
019048,001547: 40,2740           64317                           AD       R1D1                                  #  RXD4

019051,001550: 40,2743           30155                           CA       MPAC       +1                         
019052,001551: 40,2744           03306                           TC       DSPDECVN                              #  DISPLAY 2ND INTEGER (LIKE VERB AND NOUN)

019055,001554:

019059,001558:                                                                                                  #  DOES NOT FORCE TPAGREE.

019256,001755:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.

019865,002364:

Page 450 

019867,002366:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
019868,002367:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
019869,002368:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
019870,002369:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
019871,002370:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
019872,002371: 
019873,002372:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
019874,002373:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
019875,002374:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
019876,002375:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
019877,002376:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
019878,002377:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
019879,002378:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
019880,002379: 
019881,002380:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON(+=ON, +0=OFF)
019882,002381:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019883,002382:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019884,002383: 
019885,002384:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
019886,002385:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
019887,002386: 
019888,002387:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
019889,002388:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
019890,002389: 
019891,002390:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

020018,002517:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
020019,002518:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
020020,002519:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
020021,002520: 
020022,002521:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
020023,002522: 
020024,002523:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
020025,002524:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
020026,002525:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
020027,002526: 
020028,002527:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
020029,002528:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
020030,002529:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
020031,002530: 
020032,002531: 41,3353           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
020033,002532: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
020034,002533: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
020035,002534: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
020036,002535: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
020037,002536: 41,3360           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
020038,002537: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
020039,002538: 41,3362           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

020467,002966:

Page 463 

020469,002968:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
020470,002969: 
020471,002970:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
020472,002971: 
020473,002972:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
020474,002973:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
020475,002974:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
020476,002975:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
020477,002976: 
020478,002977:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
020479,002978:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
020480,002979:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
020481,002980: 
020482,002981:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
020483,002982:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
020484,002983:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
020485,002984:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
020486,002985:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
020487,002986:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
020488,002987:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
020489,002988:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
020490,002989:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
020491,002990:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
020492,002991:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
020493,002992: 
020494,002993: 40,3457           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
020495,002994: 40,3460           00006                           EXTEND                                         
020496,002995: 40,3461           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
020497,002996: 40,3462           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
020498,002997: 40,3463           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020499,002998: 40,3464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
020500,002999: 40,3465           10000                           CCS      A                                     
020501,003000: 40,3466           03475                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
020502,003001: 40,3467           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
020503,003002: 40,3470           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
020504,003003: 40,3471           03473                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
020505,003004: 40,3472           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020506,003005: 40,3473           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
020507,003006: 40,3474           20723                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
020508,003007: 40,3475           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
020509,003008: 40,3476           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
020510,003009: 40,3477           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
020511,003010: 40,3500           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
020512,003011: 40,3501           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
020513,003012: 40,3502           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020514,003013: 
020515,003014: 40,3503                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
020516,003015:

Page 464 

020518,003017:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
020519,003018:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
020520,003019:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
020521,003020:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
020522,003021:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
020523,003022: 
020524,003023:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
020525,003024:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
020526,003025:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
020527,003026: 
020528,003027:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
020529,003028:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
020530,003029: 
020531,003030:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020532,003031:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
020533,003032:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
020534,003033:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
020535,003034:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
020536,003035: 
020537,003036:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020538,003037:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
020539,003038:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
020540,003039:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
020541,003040: 
020542,003041:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
020543,003042:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
020544,003043:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
020545,003044:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
020546,003045:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
020547,003046:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
020548,003047:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
020549,003048: 
020550,003049:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
020551,003050:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
020552,003051: 
020553,003052:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
020554,003053:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
020555,003054: 
020556,003055:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
020557,003056:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
020558,003057: 
020559,003058:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
020560,003059:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
020561,003060:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
020562,003061:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
020563,003062:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
020564,003063:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
020565,003064:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
020566,003065: 
020567,003066:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 465 

020569,003068:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
020570,003069:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
020571,003070:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
020572,003071:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
020573,003072:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
020574,003073:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
020575,003074:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
020576,003075:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
020577,003076:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
020578,003077: 
020579,003078:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
020580,003079:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
020581,003080: 
020582,003081:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
020583,003082: 
020584,003083:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

020697,003196:                                                                                                  #   MONITOR BIT.
020698,003197:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
020699,003198: 
020700,003199: 
020701,003200:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
020702,003201:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020703,003202:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020704,003203:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
020705,003204:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
020706,003205: 
020707,003206: 
020708,003207:                                                                                                  #  L  TC ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
020709,003208:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
020710,003209:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
020711,003210:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020712,003211:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020713,003212:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
020714,003213:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
020715,003214:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
020716,003215:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
020717,003216:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
020718,003217: 
020719,003218: 
020720,003219:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 468 

020722,003221:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
020723,003222:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
020724,003223:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020725,003224:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
020726,003225:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
020727,003226: 
020728,003227:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
020729,003228:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
020730,003229:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
020731,003230:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
020732,003231:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
020733,003232:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
020734,003233:    4215           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
020735,003234:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020736,003235: 
020737,003236: 
020738,003237:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020739,003238: 
020740,003239:

020843,003342: 40,3526           10000                           CCS      A

020845,003344: 40,3530           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  IF CURRENT BIT = 0, RETURN TO L+3.
020846,003345: 40,3531           00002                           TC       2

020852,003351:                                                                                                  #  PRIO 30000 FOR DSPMMJB AND RETURNS TO CALLER.

020894,003393:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED), TERMINATE VERB IS EXECUTED, OR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA VERB IS
020895,003394:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IT WAKES UP JOB THAT DID TC ENDIDLE.

020898,003397:                                                                                                  #  LIGHT IF DSPLIST IS EMPTY (LEAVES KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF NOT EMPTY).
