021083,003582:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
021084,003583: 
021085,003584:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
021086,003585:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
021087,003586:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
021088,003587:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
021089,003588: 
021090,003589:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021091,003590:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
021092,003591:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
021093,003592:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
021094,003593:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021095,003594:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
021096,003595:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
021097,003596: 
021098,003597: 
021099,003598:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
021100,003599:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
021101,003600:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
021102,003601:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
021103,003602:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
021104,003603: 
021105,003604: 
021106,003605:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
021107,003606:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021108,003607:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
021109,003608:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
021110,003609:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
021111,003610: 
021112,003611: 
021113,003612:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
021114,003613:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
021115,003614:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
021116,003615: 
021117,003616: 
021118,003617:                                                                                                  #  .
021119,003618: 
021120,003619: 
021121,003620:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
021122,003621:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
021123,003622:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
021124,003623:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
021125,003624: 
021126,003625: 
021127,003626:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021128,003627:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
021129,003628:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
021130,003629:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
021131,003630:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
021132,003631:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 477 

021134,003633:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
021135,003634: 
021136,003635:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
021137,003636:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
021138,003637:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
021139,003638:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
021140,003639:    4443           10604                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
021141,003640:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
021142,003641: 
021143,003642:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
021144,003643:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
021145,003644: 
021146,003645: 04,2604                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
021147,003646: 04,2604                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021148,003647: 04,2604           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
021149,003648: 04,2605           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
021150,003649: 04,2606           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
021151,003650: 04,2607           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
021152,003651: 04,2610           30001                           CA       L                                     
021153,003652: 04,2611           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
021154,003653: 04,2612           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
021155,003654: 
021156,003655: 
021157,003656:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
021158,003657:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
021159,003658:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
021160,003659:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
021161,003660:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
021162,003661: 
021163,003662:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
021164,003663:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021165,003664:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
021166,003665:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
021167,003666:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
021168,003667:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
021169,003668:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
021170,003669:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
021171,003670:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
021172,003671:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
021173,003672:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
021174,003673:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
021175,003674:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
021176,003675: 
021177,003676:

021329,003828:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
021330,003829:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
021331,003830:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
021332,003831:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
021333,003832:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
021334,003833:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
